BybitAdapter ë©”ì„œë“œ ë‚´ë¶€ì—ì„œ ë§¤í•‘ ì‚¬ìš©\n\nì˜ˆì‹œ:\n\n```python\nclass BybitAdapter:\n    ...\n\n    def get_price(self, symbol: str) -> float:\n        bybit_symbol = _to_bybit_symbol(symbol)\n        # ì—¬ê¸°ì„œ Bybitìš© ì‹¤ì œ API í˜¸ì¶œ\n        # ì˜ˆ: self.client.get_ticker(bybit_symbol)\n        ...\n\n    def place_order(self, symbol: str, side: str, qty: float, order_type: str = \"MARKET\"):\n        bybit_symbol = _to_bybit_symbol(symbol)\n        bybit_side = SIDE_MAP.get(side.upper(), side)\n        bybit_type = ORDER_TYPE_MAP.get(order_type.upper(), order_type)\n\n        # ì˜ˆì‹œ: self.client.place_order(symbol=bybit_symbol, side=bybit_side, qty=qty, type=bybit_type)\n        ...\n```\n\n**í•µì‹¬ í¬ì¸íŠ¸:**  \n- **ì™¸ë¶€(ì „ëµÂ·realtime_loop)ëŠ” í•­ìƒ Binance ê¸°ì¤€ ì¸í„°í˜ì´ìŠ¤ & ì‹¬ë³¼ë§Œ ë³¸ë‹¤.**  \n- BybitAdapterëŠ” ê·¸ê±¸ **ì•ˆì—ì„œë§Œ** Bybit ìŠ¤íƒ€ì¼ë¡œ ë°”ê¿”ì¤€ë‹¤.\n\n---\n\n## â‘¤ `get_exchange_adapter()`ì—ì„œ ê³µí†µ íƒ€ì… ì‚¬ìš© í™•ì¸\n\n### 5-1. `src/exchange/__init__.py` ì—´ê¸°\n\n1. âš  ì—†ë‹¤ë©´: pip install ccxt\n\nfrom .exchange_base import ExchangeAdapter\n\n\nclass BinanceAdapter:\n    \"\"\"\n    Binance ì‹¤ì „ êµ¬í˜„ì²´.\n    - ExchangeAdapter ì¸í„°í˜ì´ìŠ¤ë¥¼ ê¸°ì¤€ìœ¼ë¡œ í•œë‹¤.\n    - ì‹¬ë³¼ì€ ê¸°ë³¸ì ìœ¼ë¡œ \"BTCUSDT\" í˜•ì‹ ë˜ëŠ” \"BTC/USDT\" ë‘˜ ë‹¤ í—ˆìš©.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(\n        self,\n        api_key: Optional[str] = None,\n        api_secret: Optional[str] = None,\n    ) -> None:\n        api_key = api_key or os.getenv(\"BINANCE_API_KEY\", \"\")\n        api_secret = api_secret or os.getenv(\"BINANCE_API_SECRET\", \"\")\n\n        self.client = ccxt.binance(\n            {\n                \"apiKey\": api_key or None,\n                \"secret\": api_secret or None,\n                \"enableRateLimit\": True,\n            }\n        )\n\n    # -------------------------\n    # ë‚´ë¶€ í—¬í¼\n    # -------------------------\n    @staticmethod\n    def _norm_symbol(symbol: str) -> str:\n        \"\"\"\n        \"BTCUSDT\" / \"BTC/USDT\" ë‘˜ ë‹¤ ë“¤ì–´ì˜¤ë©´\n        ccxt í‘œì¤€ ì‹¬ë³¼ \"BTC/USDT\" ë¡œ ë§ì¶˜ë‹¤.\n        \"\"\"\n        if \"/\" in symbol:\n            return symbol\n        if symbol.endswith(\"USDT\"):\n            return symbol.replace(\"USDT\", \"/USDT\")\n        return symbol\n\n    # \"buy\" / \"sell\"\n        order_type = order_type.lower()  # \"market\" / \"limit\"\n\n        params = kwargs.get(\"params\") or {}\n        if \"params\" in kwargs:\n            kwargs.pop(\"params\")\n\n        return self.client.create_order(\n            symbol=s,\n            side=side,\n            type=order_type,\n            amount=qty,\n            params=params,\n            **kwargs,\n        )\n\n    def cancel_order(self, symbol: str, order_id: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        s = self._norm_symbol(symbol)\n        return self.client.cancel_order(id=order_id, symbol=s)\n\n    def get_position(self, symbol: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        \"\"\"\n        Spot ê¸°ì¤€: í¬ì§€ì…˜ ê°œë…ì´ ì—†ìœ¼ë¯€ë¡œ\n        - ì”ê³  ê¸°ì¤€ìœ¼ë¡œ size/sideë¥¼ ì¶”ì •í•˜ê±°ë‚˜\n        - ìš°ì„  flat ì²˜ë¦¬ (í•„ìš” ì‹œ í™•ì¥)\n        \"\"\"\n        return {\n            \"symbol\": symbol,\n            \"size\": 0.0,\n            \"side\": \"flat\",\n        }\n```\n\n> ccxtê°€ ì—†ë‹¤ë©´ `requirements.local.txt` ì— `ccxt` ì¶”ê°€í•˜ê³  `pip install -r ...` í•œ ë²ˆ í•´ì¤˜ì•¼ í•´.\n\n---\n\n## â‘£ `bybit_adapter.py` ìƒì„± + Binance ë§¤í•‘\n\n### 4-1. ìƒˆ íŒŒì¼ ë§Œë“¤ê¸° (í´ë¦­)\n\n- VSCode ì™¼ìª½ íƒìƒ‰ê¸°  \n  â†’ `src` â†’ `exchange` í´ë” **ìš°í´ë¦­**  \n  â†’ **New File** í´ë¦­  \n  â†’ íŒŒì¼ ì´ë¦„ì— `bybit_adapter.py` ì…ë ¥ í›„ ì—”í„°\n\n### 4-2. ì•„ë˜ ì½”ë“œ ì „ì²´ ë¶™ì—¬ë„£ê¸° â†’ `Ctrl + S`\n\n```python\n# src/exchange/bybit_adapter.py\n\nimport os\nfrom typing import Dict, Any, Optional\n\nimport ccxt  # Binanceì™€ ë™ì¼ ë¼ì´ë¸ŒëŸ¬ë¦¬ ì‚¬ìš©\n\nfrom .exchange_base import ExchangeAdapter\n\n\n# Binance ê¸°ì¤€ ì‹¬ë³¼ â†’ Bybit(ccxt) ì‹¬ë³¼ ë§¤í•‘\nSYMBOL_MAP: Dict[str, str] = {\n    \"BTCUSDT\": \"BTC/USDT\",\n    \"ETHUSDT\": \"ETH/USDT\",\n    # í•„ìš” ì‹œ ì—¬ê¸° ê³„ì† ì¶”ê°€\n}\n\n\ndef _to_bybit_symbol(symbol: str) -> str:\n    if \"/\" in symbol:\n        return symbol\n    return SYMBOL_MAP.get(symbol, symbol.replace(\"USDT\", \"/USDT\"))\n\n\nclass BybitAdapter:\n    \"\"\"\n    Bybit ì‹¤ì „ êµ¬í˜„ì²´.\n    - ì™¸ë¶€ì—ì„œëŠ” Binance ê¸°ì¤€ ì¸í„°í˜ì´ìŠ¤/ì‹¬ë³¼ì„ ì“´ë‹¤.\n    - ë‚´ë¶€ì—ì„œë§Œ Bybit ì‹¬ë³¼/íŒŒë¼ë¯¸í„°ë¡œ ë§¤í•‘í•œë‹¤.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(\n        self,\n        api_key: Optional[str] = None,\n        api_secret: Optional[str] = None,\n    ) -> None:\n        api_key = api_key or os.getenv(\"BYBIT_API_KEY\", \"\")\n        api_secret = api_secret or os.getenv(\"BYBIT_API_SECRET\", \"\")\n\n        self.client = ccxt.bybit(\n            {\n                \"apiKey\": api_key or None,\n                \"secret\": api_secret or None,\n                \"enableRateLimit\": True,\n            }\n        )\n\n    # -------------------------\n    # í‘œì¤€ ì¸í„°í˜ì´ìŠ¤ êµ¬í˜„\n    # -------------------------\n    def get_realtime_price(self, symbol: str) -> float:\n        return self.get_price(symbol)\n\n    def get_price(self, symbol: str) -> float:\n        s = _to_bybit_symbol(symbol)\n        ticker = self.client.fetch_ticker(s)\n        return float(ticker[\"last\"])\n\n    def place_order(\n        self,\n        symbol: str,\n        side: str,\n        qty: float,\n        order_type: str = \"MARKET\",\n        **kwargs: Any,\n    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        s = _to_bybit_symbol(symbol)\n        side = side.lower()\n        order_type = order_type.lower()\n\n        params = kwargs.get(\"params\") or {}\n        if \"params\" in kwargs:\n            kwargs.pop(\"params\")\n\n        return self.client.create_order(\n            symbol=s,\n            side=side,\n            type=order_type,\n            amount=qty,\n            params=params,\n            **kwargs,\n        )\n\n    def cancel_order(self, symbol: str, order_id: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        s = _to_bybit_symbol(symbol)\n        return self.client.cancel_order(id=order_id, symbol=s)\n\n    def get_position(self, symbol: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:\n        # TODO: Bybit í¬ì§€ì…˜ API ì—°ë™ ì‹œ í™•ì¥\n        return {\n            \"symbol\": symbol,\n            \"size\": 0.0,\n            \"side\": \"flat\",\n        }\n```\n\n> ì´ë ‡ê²Œ í•˜ë©´ ì „ëµ ìª½ì—ì„œëŠ” ê³„ì† `\"BTCUSDT\"` ë§Œ ì“°ê³ ,  \n> ì‹¤ì œë¡œëŠ” Binance/Bybit ê°ì `\"BTC/USDT\"` ë¡œ ì•Œì•„ì„œ ë§¤í•‘ëœë‹¤.\n\n---\n\n## â‘¤ `mock.py`ëŠ” ì¼ë‹¨ ê·¸ëŒ€ë¡œ ë‘ê³ , ì´ë¦„ë§Œ í™•ì¸\n\n- VSCodeì—ì„œ `src/exchange/mock.py` ë”ë¸”í´ë¦­í•´ì„œ  \n  **ì‹¤ì œ ì–´ëŒ‘í„° í´ë˜ìŠ¤ ì´ë¦„(ì˜ˆ: `MockExchangeAdapter`, `MockAdapter` ë“±)** ë§Œ ê¸°ì–µí•´ ë‘¬.\n- ì´ ì´ë¦„ì´ ë‹¤ìŒ ë‹¨ê³„ `__init__.py` ì—ì„œ í•„ìš”í•´.\n\n---\n\n## â‘¥ `__init__.py` ì •ë¦¬ â€“ get_exchange_adapter í†µí•©\n\n### 6-1. í´ë¦­ ê²½ë¡œ\n\n- VSCode ì™¼ìª½ íƒìƒ‰ê¸°  \n  â†’ `src` â†’ `exchange` â†’ `__init__.py` ë”ë¸”í´ë¦­\n\n### 6-2. íŒŒì¼ ë‚´ìš©ì„ ì•„ë˜ì²˜ëŸ¼ ì •ë¦¬ (ê¸°ì¡´ ë‚´ìš©ì€ ë®ì–´ì¨ë„ ë¨)\n\n```python\n# src/exchange/__init__.py\n\nimport os\n\nfrom .exchange_base import ExchangeAdapter\nfrom .binance_adapter import BinanceAdapter\nfrom .bybit_adapter import BybitAdapter\nfrom .mock import MockExchangeAdapter  # âš  mock.py ì•ˆ í´ë˜ìŠ¤ ì´ë¦„ì— ë§ê²Œ ìˆ˜ì •\n\n\ndef get_exchange_adapter() -> ExchangeAdapter:\n    \"\"\"\n    EXCHANGE í™˜ê²½ë³€ìˆ˜ì— ë”°ë¼ ì ì ˆí•œ ì–´ëŒ‘í„°ë¥¼ ë°˜í™˜í•œë‹¤.\n\n    EXCHANGE=binance  â†’ BinanceAdapter\n    EXCHANGE=bybit    â†’ BybitAdapter\n    ê·¸ ì™¸ / ë¯¸ì„¤ì •     â†’ MockExchangeAdapter\n    \"\"\"\n    ex = os.getenv(\"EXCHANGE\", \"mock\").lower()\n\n    if ex == \"binance\":\n        return BinanceAdapter()\n    if ex == \"bybit\":\n        return BybitAdapter()\n\n    #
